## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="abf01-1143">Атрибуты Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="abf01-1143">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>
